posted:Posted June 30, 2021
msg:We were looking for an inexpensive hotel in Yalong Bay area close to the sea. Initially we were a bit hesitant to book Aegean because some reviews were not great, but in the end we were very happy! It was more beautiful than in the photos. 
Some guests mentioned that the amenities were old, but we found everything in good condition, cozy, clean, and functioning.
The atmosphere is very relaxing, there is a big pool, places to sit in the hotel park, and the beach (it's a public beach, not private, but clean) is just a minute away.
The staff was very nice, upgraded our rooms and accommodated late check-out.
Sea-view rooms are spacious, bright, and have a big balcony.
The room has a modern washing machine, oven and hotplate, as well as a big fridge, very convenient.
It's very quiet and family friendly, best for when you just want to be lazy and relax.
There are restaurants and shops less than 2 km away, and you can get everything delivered fast.
Definitely would stay again.
